data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;p&gt;I really wanted to say something, what most would call, mean this morning on someone&#039;s FB page. Not because they deserved it but because it was the truth that they have come to realize and admitted. I wanted to let them know I agree with them but thought it would be hurtful and not needed. Everyone wants to be supportive and confirming of your desires and lately no one has the balls to say to their friends the truth. So here we go my &quot;friends&quot;, message me (no need to go public) what you like about my photography and what you don&#039;t like. I only get better by real criticism and not weak pandering to my ego.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;form rel="async" class="commentable_item collapsed_comments" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;C&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div class="_5pcn fwb" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;k&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;a href="/mindfulschools/photos/a.203073253066340.49931.165948186778847/598713920168936/?type=1&amp;fref=nf"&gt;Mindful Schools&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="mtm _5pco" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a1aa0b533ee8793500990" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;A psychologist walked around a room while teaching stress management to an audience. As she raised a glass of water, everyone expected they&#039;d be asked the &quot;half&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt; empty or half full&quot; question. Instead, with a smile on her face, she inquired: &quot;How heavy is this glass of water?&quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class="text_exposed_show"&gt;&lt;p&gt; Answers called out ranged from 8 oz. to 20 oz.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; She replied, &quot;The absolute weight doesn&#039;t matter. It depends on how long I hold it. If I hold it for a minute, it&#039;s not a problem. If I hold it for an hour, I&#039;ll have an ache in my arm. If I hold it for a day, my arm will feel numb and paralyzed. In each case, the weight of the glass doesn&#039;t change, but the longer I hold it, the heavier it becomes.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; She continued, &quot;The stresses and worries in life are like that glass of water. Think about them for a while and nothing happens. Think about them a bit longer and they begin to hurt. And if you think about them all day long, you will feel paralyzed  incapable of doing anything.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Remember to put the glass down.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; (Courtesy of Jimmy Harmon)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt; &lt;span class="text_exposed_link"&gt;&lt;a class="see_more_link" onclick="var func = function(e) &#123; e.preventDefault(); &#125;;
